Description: Drosophila: entries, gene names and cross-references to
             FlyBase
Name:        fly.txt
Release:     2016_07 of 06-Jul-2016

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

More information on Drosophila, its  genome, proteome, biology and genetics,
is available from the following WWW servers:

FlyBase      : http://flybase.org/

For each Drosophila entry in Swiss-Prot we provide the following information:

1) Primary gene name

   We indicate as the primary gene name, the gene symbol  currently in use
   in FlyBase.

2) Drosophila FlyBase species 'code'

   If a sequence does not originate from Drosophila melanogaster, then the
   species of origin is indicated using the  FlyBase  four letter code for
   that  species.   Example, Dvir stands for Drosophila virilis. All these
   codes refer to Drosophila species with the exception of the following:

   Camo for Chymomyza amoena
   Salb for Scaptomyza albovittata
   Ztub for Zaprionus tuberculatus

3) Swiss-Prot entry name

4) Swiss-Prot primary accession number

5) FlyBase gene accession number

   If more than one Swiss-Prot entries are linked to the same FlyBase entry
   than only the FlyBase gene accession number is only indicated once. This
   occurs when multiple entries are created due to alternative  splicing or
   when a transposable element encodes for a number of putative proteins.
